`(T - 352.16) * (-0.5450 + 1.5180*epsilon^0.6262)`

Expanding:
`-0.5450*T + 191.91 + 1.5180*T*epsilon^0.6262 - 534.58*epsilon^0.6262`

So the GT is: `T*(-0.5450 + 1.5180*epsilon^0.6262) + (191.91 - 534.58*epsilon^0.6262)`

This can be written as: `T*c_a*epsilon^c_b + T*c_c + c_d*epsilon^c_b + c_e`

Let me check candidates that have terms like `T*epsilon^c` and `T` and `epsilon^c` and constant terms.

**Candidate 18:** `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*sin(c3*epsilon + c4) + c5*epsilon + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon + c9))`

**Candidate 8:** `T*c0 + T*c1*sin(c2*epsilon + c3) + c4*sqrt(c5 + epsilon**2) + c6 + c7*epsilon**c8`

**Candidate 15:** `T**c0*c1*epsilon**c2 + c3*epsilon**2 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon + c9))`

**Candidate 47:** `c0*epsilon**2 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*log(T*c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + 1) + c6*epsilon**c7*log(T*c8 + 1)`
